data-w-id="c4514580-fbd2-4d79-e2c3-8fb41ba7aa17" style="opacity: 0;" class="vr_par1 border">Surgical VR training simulations made by Ghost Medical using the Wraith-VR surgery platform allows you to demonstrate your instrumentation, devices, and procedure to doctors all over the world.</p><div data-w-id="63fbeb74-be0e-ec61-20d1-27042817a1ff" class="surgerydiv"><h3 harming patients.
